# Tier-1 Catalog Round-Trip ‚Äî Automated Test Log

> Generated by `scripts/catalog-sweep.ts` (Sprint 4, decision 25). Every test round-trips a
> user-style concept built FROM a kept criterion's name and asserts it grounds back to that id.
> The label is by-construction (the source catalog row), so it is E8-clean. Same format as
> [EvaledQueries.md](EvaledQueries.md): each entry logs the concept, its source criterion, what
> it grounded to, and a correct/incorrect status. **One entry per test, rewritten each run.**

## Summary

```
Catalog round-trip: 2485/2486 pass (100.0%) [clean 2460 + twin 25 + narrowed 0] | ceilings: 3627 absent, 2437 quarantined (0 leaks)
verbatim floor: clean 2460, twin 25, narrowed 0, none 0, below 0, ambiguous 0, wrong-id 1, wrong-bucket 0
paraphrase batch: 14/36 pass (38.9%) ‚Äî clean 8, twin 0, narrowed 6, none 1, below 11, ambiguous 5, wrong-id 5, wrong-bucket 0
aliases (growth guard): 175 merged (curated + derived)
```

- **clean** ‚Äî grounded back to the source id at tier `confident|variants` (a pass).
- **twin** ‚Äî grounded to the SAME market under a sibling id (settlement/register duplicate) ‚Äî a pass.
- **narrowed** ‚Äî the source id is present in a non-confident `ambiguous`/`shortlist` set (the executor clarifies, but grounding didn't lose it) ‚Äî a pass.
- **below** ‚Äî sub-threshold `shortlist` (recall floor) NOT containing the source; **none** ‚Äî abstained below FLOOR.
- **ambiguous** ‚Äî a different-core near-tie; **wrong-id** ‚Äî confident on the wrong sibling;
  **wrong-bucket** ‚Äî confident on a market in the other subject bucket.
- **absent** = referenced category ids with no criterion row (a data-feed gap, not a bug).
  **quarantined** = per-player pre-baked rows dropped at build; the sweep asserts **0 leak** into results.
